 description ---> Director Personal InsuranceWestland Insurance GroupVictoria, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONVictoria, BCPOSTED4 days agoDirector Personal Insurance Kelowna, BC, Canada • Surrey, BC, Canada • Vancouver, BC, Canada • Victoria, BC, Canada • Virtual Req #833  Wednesday, April 20, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Director, Personal Insurance working remotely anywhere in British Columbia. In the leadership position of Director, Personal Insurance you will represent Westland to the market and implement and support Westland's key initiatives and goals. You will bring together strong sales, coaching, and technical skills to support the branches in achieving the goals of the company, our clients, and employees. What we offer:  A highly customer centric organization and position focused on service first  High-growth company environment with great opportunity for development  Competitive compensation structure and bonuses  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: Providing leadership to Regional Sales Managers across your respective region, this role is responsible for sales and growth, people development and talent management, sales leadership, sales management, and business plan execution. You will drive sales performance and revenue growth through the art of advisory based sales coaching. The Director, Personal Lines Insurance: Works closely with the People & Performance Team to develop and execute Talent Management programs within the region. Provides their Regional Sales Managers coaching on managing attraction, recruitment, retention and engagement strategies throughout their regions.  Develops and regularly reviews key performance metrics and implements actions to address deficiencies and enhance successes.  Accountable to achieve Policy In Force (PIF) and Customer count growth targets annually.  Responsible for the recruitment and development of Regional Sales Managers, ensuring to work towards having a pipeline of talent for vacancies and succession planning both internally and externally.  Ensures the ongoing development of employees; team and individual goals are set, coaching and feedback is being provided consistently and managers are identifying career development opportunities based on interests and strengths.  Accountable for having an increased presence in the branches and communities, with minimum weekly sales meetings and monthly visits by Regional Sales Managers and themselves.  Participates and contributes as a member of the Retail Leadership team to provide input into and executing upon the overall plan. Formulates the development of their respective Region's business plan complete with sales targets and tactics that will meet or exceed the budget for personal lines.  Responsible for the achievement of a strong, proactive sales and service culture through motivational leadership and coaching. Learns and teaches the art of coaching. If necessary, works with Training team on developing and/or sourcing out the most effective training programs.  Works with Regional Sales Managers to develop and implement branch sales activities.  Responsible for profitability within their respective Region by ensuring sales targets are met, teams are effectively managing salary budgets and forecasting of resourcing requirements.  Convenes and leads regular meetings within their Region to cascade key information and ensure initiatives are implemented effectively. Manages any change management impacts with the implementation of new programs or initiatives.  Collaborates with other lines of business through reciprocity of referrals to lead to new members, customers, and product sales.  Stays abreast of competitive, environmental and industry trends that may impact marketing position and member satisfaction; sets direction; focuses resources and executes plans to develop and grow the business.  Fosters and maintains strong relationships with Westland's key business partners, primarily, the Insurance companies through which the company writes business.  Maintains a high level of current industry knowledge and actively participates in professional associations related to insurance such as Insurance Brokers Association of BC, staying at the forefront of the profession. Support charitable organizations through company and industry events.  Supports special projects and key initiatives as directed by the Retail Operations leaders.  For new acquisitions, ensures appropriate training and staffing levels to support the. Provides support for salary and benefits harmonization under the guidance of the VP Personal Insurance.  Travel as required. Here's what you bring:  Minimum of 5 years' management / leadership experience.  Demonstrated effective leadership within the insurance industry, applying proactive sales and service environment.  Proven results in developing, coaching and leading a team.  Demonstrated commitment to excellence in the insurance industry and the ability to differentiate Westland in the marketplace.  Demonstrated ability to exceed business results and inspire teams to perform within an extremely competitive environment.  Demonstrated ability to execute tactical plans that link to the operating and strategic plans of the business.  High level of personal and professional integrity with exceptional communication and interpersonal skills.  Post-secondary education in Business Administration, or other related field preferred.  Achieved highest possible P&C Insurance License, working on or achieved CAIB or CIP designation. Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process. You will bring together strong sales, coaching, and technical skills to support the branches in achieving the goals of the company, our clients, and employees. What we offer:  A highly customer centric organization and position focused on service first  High-growth company environment with great opportunity for development  Competitive compensation structure and bonuses  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: Providing leadership to Regional Sales Managers across your respective region, this role is responsible for sales and growth, people development and talent management, sales leadership, sales management, and business plan execution. Accountable to achieve Policy In Force (PIF) and Customer count growth targets annually.  Responsible for the recruitment and development of Regional Sales Managers, ensuring to work towards having a pipeline of talent for vacancies and succession planning both internally and externally. Accountable for having an increased presence in the branches and communities, with minimum weekly sales meetings and monthly visits by Regional Sales Managers and themselves.  Participates and contributes as a member of the Retail Leadership team to provide input into and executing upon the overall plan. Formulates the development of their respective Region's business plan complete with sales targets and tactics that will meet or exceed the budget for personal lines.  Responsible for the achievement of a strong, proactive sales and service culture through motivational leadership and coaching. Learns and teaches the art of coaching. If necessary, works with Training team on developing and/or sourcing out the most effective training programs.  Works with Regional Sales Managers to develop and implement branch sales activities.  Responsible for profitability within their respective Region by ensuring sales targets are met, teams are effectively managing salary budgets and forecasting of resourcing requirements.  Convenes and leads regular meetings within their Region to cascade key information and ensure initiatives are implemented effectively. Manages any change management impacts with the implementation of new programs or initiatives.  Collaborates with other lines of business through reciprocity of referrals to lead to new members, customers, and product sales.  Stays abreast of competitive, environmental and industry trends that may impact marketing position and member satisfaction; sets direction; focuses resources and executes plans to develop and grow the business.  Fosters and maintains strong relationships with Westland's key business partners, primarily, the Insurance companies through which the company writes business.  Maintains a high level of current industry knowledge and actively participates in professional associations related to insurance such as Insurance Brokers Association of BC, staying at the forefront of the profession. Support charitable organizations through company and industry events.  Supports special projects and key initiatives as directed by the Retail Operations leaders.  For new acquisitions, ensures appropriate training and staffing levels to support the. Provides support for salary and benefits harmonization under the guidance of the VP Personal Insurance.  Travel as required. Here's what you bring:  Minimum of 5 years' management / leadership experience.  Demonstrated effective leadership within the insurance industry, applying proactive sales and service environment.  Proven results in developing, coaching and leading a team.  Demonstrated commitment to excellence in the insurance industry and the ability to differentiate Westland in the marketplace.  Demonstrated ability to exceed business results and inspire teams to perform within an extremely competitive environment.  Demonstrated ability to execute tactical plans that link to the operating and strategic plans of the business.  High level of personal and professional integrity with exceptional communication and interpersonal skills.  Post-secondary education in Business Administration, or other related field preferred.  Achieved highest possible P&C Insurance License, working on or achieved CAIB or CIP designation.  description ---> Branch ManagerWestland Insurance GroupDelta, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONDelta, BCPOSTED2 days agoBranch Manager  Tsawwassen (Tsawwassen Center), BC, 1288 56th Street, Delta, British Columbia, Canada Req #591  Friday, April 22, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd. has an exciting opportunity for a Branch Manager in Tsawwassen, BC at our Tsawwassen Shopping Centre. Are you looking for growth in your career, building a team, developing and mentoring staff? If so, we want to hear from you. We are looking for a career minded individual who is focused on expanding their management experience in a rapidly growing organization. What we offer:  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: This position provides leadership to team members within a branch. They are knowledgeable with technical insurance products (personal lines and auto) and have the management skills to support the team in achieving the goals of the company, our clients and employees. In this role you'll: • Achieve targets within the sales and marketing plans  • Conduct monthly sales/production meetings and performance meetings with team members  • Provide guidance and support to sales agents to ensure they attain expected targets  • Develop and deliver a sales and marketing plan for their branch  • Prepare sales and expense budgets with an emphasis on growth and profitability  • Handle member/client concerns effectively or accelerating to executive level as required  • Handle branch administration including operational support for agency staff  • Hire, develop, coach and mentor agents and staff  • Demonstrate leadership abilities and effectively manage changing priorities  • Collaborate with other business unit managers to attain standards and operational levels Here's what you bring: • 5 years of industry experience  • Post-secondary degree or diploma is preferred  • Previous people management/leadership experience  • Insurance broker level 2 license is a must. CAIB and/or CIP are an asset  • Proven results in developing and leading a team  • A natural ability at building authentic customer relationships  • Excellent time management skills and the ability to multi-task  • Demonstrated business acumen Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process.  description ---> Facilities ManagerWestland Insurance GroupVancouver, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONVancouver, BCPOSTED4 days agoFacilities Manager Vancouver, BC, Canada Req #817  Wednesday, April 20, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Facilities Manager working remotely anywhere in Canada. As Facilities Manager you will represent Westland Insurance Group Ltd. and be responsible for supporting Westland locations with arranging service calls, identifying and selecting vendors, and organizing information on Westland's various facilities for ease of future access and follow-up. You will play an essential role in supporting Westland's key initiatives and continuing growth. What we offer:  A highly customer centric organization and position focused on service first  High-growth company environment with great opportunity for development  Competitive compensation structure and bonuses  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity:  Gather, collate, and manage facilities related information on Westland branches and corporate offices.  Manage the creation and maintenance spreadsheets, Smartsheets, Service now & Share point.  Update individual office location data as locations close or new locations are added; this includes updating addresses, contact information, trades and suppliers, floor plans, permits, etc.  Create and manage online smartsheet facilities information forms.  Manage and maintain ServiceNow facilities tickets submitted by branches.  Update/adapt ServiceNow and Smartsheet forms as deemed required.  Seek out trades, vendors and suppliers; research and identify trades and suppliers in all regions we operate.  Review, negotiate and sign various vendor contracts such as janitorial, security, alarms, HVAC, and pest control etc...  Coordinate and support access for installations or service calls such as security, water filtration, shred services, janitorial, etc.  Manage installations, maintenance & removal of alarm and security for all locations. including individual alarm codes for staff and all after hours alarm response calls.  Manage and coordinate preventative and cyclical maintenance such as mechanical, landscaping, snow removal, water filter changes, fire safety, etc.  Contact and liaise between landlords, property managers, and subtenants to address complaints or repairs required.  Approving Facilities invoices in Concur on a weekly recuring basis.  Managing internal departments/external vendors to achieve Facilities department goals and initiatives.  Communicates various events or tasks to internal and external clients via phone or email.  Provide support to Westland renovation and construction project teams.  Manage/update service providers to support new builds, renovations, merge, and acquisitions.  Manage onboarding of new facilities staff. Here's what you bring:  Proven experience in a facilities management role, ideally within a retail/branch organization  High level of experience understanding/reviewing vendor contracts.  Ability to read plans and edit PDF's  Keen Knowledge of all Construction and Repairs  Previous experience in a role managing and consolidating large amounts of information in Excel or Smartsheet  High level of proficiency in MS Office (Excel, Word, Outlook etc.)  Experience with Smartsheets, Service Now and SharePoint is an assett  Excellent organizational and problem-solving skills, and a service-oriented mindset  Excellent time management and the ability to juggle multiple priorities  Strong communication skills including writing and editing  Strong attention to detail and accuracy and demonstrated ability to execute work promptly and efficiently  Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce.  description ---> Property Filed AdjusterWestland Insurance GroupVernon, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONVernon, BCPOSTED4 days agoProperty Filed Adjuster  Vernon, BC, Canada Req #512  Wednesday, April 20, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Property Field Adjuster working remotely and covering claims primarily in Kelowna, Vernon, and surrounding areas. This is a great opportunity and will be a home based position with daily travel required. What we offer:  Competitive salary  Vehicle Allowance  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: As a Property Field Adjuster with Westland, you will be contributing to our goal of delivering an exceptional claims experience to our clients by meeting with them and assisting them through the claims process. In this role you'll: • Investigate commercial lines and personal lines property insurance claims with insureds, third parties and other related parties in order to obtain facts and information  • Review facts, policy coverages, expert reports and case law to make decisions on coverage, claim value and settlement  • Manage and direct Restoration Contractors to ensure best practices are being followed for property restoration, and that costs are in line with work required  • Responsible for data accuracy, issuance of payments to insureds, vendors and other related parties to a claim  • Manage and direct other claim related experts such as Engineers and Legal Counsel  • Responsible for providing exemplary client service and keeping all related parties informed of the claims process and status Here's what you bring: • 5+ years of multi-line adjusting experience, with 2+ years of field work in property claims adjudication  • Insurance Broker Level 2 license and/or CIP designation  • Valid Driver's License  • Community College or University Degree  • Strong background in residential and commercial property insurance  • Ability to work independently with excellent time management and organizational skills  • Effective written and verbal communication abilities  • Good knowledge of building construction and restoration practices  • Computer proficiency with an ability to adapt easily to new computer programs Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process.  position ----> Support Specialist - IT Service Desk
 company ---> Westland Insurance Group
 description ---> Support Specialist - IT Service DeskWestland Insurance GroupSurrey, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONSurrey, BCPOSTED3 days agoSupport Specialist - IT Service Desk Surrey (Head Office), BC, 2121 160th St #200, Surrey, British Columbia, Canada Req #845  Thursday, April 21, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Support Specialist- IT Service Desk in Surrey, BC at our Surrey Head office. This is a great opportunity to join our IT Operations team.What we offer Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programsThe Opportunity: The Support Specialist is an integral member of the IT team and is responsible for ensuring that incidents relating to in-house computing systems are recorded and resolved by means of troubleshooting problems, advising on appropriate actions, or redirecting to appropriate resources using the IT Service Management System. In this role you'll:  Form part of a Service Desk team, acting as a single point of contact to communicate, manage and resolve IT incidents (break/fix) and fulfill service requests  Provide technical phone/email/desk-side support for internal IT customers  Provide level 1 and 2 phone/chat/email/desk-side support for our technology systems  Participate in IT customer projects including office moves, infrastructure deployments, and cloud services  Update, create and maintain support documentation  Add users to a network and assign and update security permissions on the network  Responsible for time allocation/prioritization, task management, and client follow up  Support users on the proper use of hardware and software  Document, track, and monitor tickets in the ticketing system to ensure timely resolution  Work as part of a team in a structured environment with defined targets and deliverables  Ability to prioritize and quickly turnaround escalated / expedited user requests  Ability to set up/modify/remove user access for a wide variety of applications  Troubleshoot/investigate issues related to laptops, desktops, printers, VOIP phones, etc. and liaise with other technical teams to resolve problems  Ability to provide real time support to a wide variety of technology users  Perform other duties as required to deliver exceptional service and support Here's what you bring: Minimum 3 years' experience in a Service Desk role  Experience with ServiceNow is considered a strong asset  Knowledge related to technology/computer science field normally attained through completion of a degree/diploma. Certification in A+, Help Desk Professional, ITIL foundations preferred or an equivalent combination of education, training, and experience  Experience providing user support in a Microsoft Active Directory environment  Proficiency in the use of remote desktop management and support tools  Experience in workstation configuration and support of desktop PCs  Experience in troubleshooting issues for Windows 10, MS Office 2010 and Office 365 and Adobe applications  Ensures process consistency and commitment to customer service excellence  Strong attention to detail and accuracy is a must  Enjoys working in a team environment but also can work independently  Demonstrates analytical, organizational and problem-solving aptitude  Excellent written and verbal communication skills  Ability to learn new technologies quickly  Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process.  description ---> Branch ManagerWestland Insurance GroupDelta, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONDelta, BCPOSTED2 days agoBranch Manager  Tsawwassen (Tsawwassen Center), BC, 1288 56th Street, Delta, British Columbia, Canada Req #591  Friday, April 22, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd. has an exciting opportunity for a Branch Manager in Tsawwassen, BC at our Tsawwassen Shopping Centre. Are you looking for growth in your career, building a team, developing and mentoring staff? If so, we want to hear from you. We are looking for a career minded individual who is focused on expanding their management experience in a rapidly growing organization. What we offer:  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: This position provides leadership to team members within a branch. They are knowledgeable with technical insurance products (personal lines and auto) and have the management skills to support the team in achieving the goals of the company, our clients and employees. In this role you'll: • Achieve targets within the sales and marketing plans  • Conduct monthly sales/production meetings and performance meetings with team members  • Provide guidance and support to sales agents to ensure they attain expected targets  • Develop and deliver a sales and marketing plan for their branch  • Prepare sales and expense budgets with an emphasis on growth and profitability  • Handle member/client concerns effectively or accelerating to executive level as required  • Handle branch administration including operational support for agency staff  • Hire, develop, coach and mentor agents and staff  • Demonstrate leadership abilities and effectively manage changing priorities  • Collaborate with other business unit managers to attain standards and operational levels Here's what you bring: • 5 years of industry experience  • Post-secondary degree or diploma is preferred  • Previous people management/leadership experience  • Insurance broker level 2 license is a must. CAIB and/or CIP are an asset  • Proven results in developing and leading a team  • A natural ability at building authentic customer relationships  • Excellent time management skills and the ability to multi-task  • Demonstrated business acumen Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process.  description ---> Facilities ManagerWestland Insurance GroupVancouver, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONVancouver, BCPOSTED4 days agoFacilities Manager Vancouver, BC, Canada Req #817  Wednesday, April 20, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Facilities Manager working remotely anywhere in Canada. As Facilities Manager you will represent Westland Insurance Group Ltd. and be responsible for supporting Westland locations with arranging service calls, identifying and selecting vendors, and organizing information on Westland's various facilities for ease of future access and follow-up. You will play an essential role in supporting Westland's key initiatives and continuing growth. What we offer:  A highly customer centric organization and position focused on service first  High-growth company environment with great opportunity for development  Competitive compensation structure and bonuses  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity:  Gather, collate, and manage facilities related information on Westland branches and corporate offices.  Manage the creation and maintenance spreadsheets, Smartsheets, Service now & Share point.  Update individual office location data as locations close or new locations are added; this includes updating addresses, contact information, trades and suppliers, floor plans, permits, etc.  Create and manage online smartsheet facilities information forms.  Manage and maintain ServiceNow facilities tickets submitted by branches.  Update/adapt ServiceNow and Smartsheet forms as deemed required.  Seek out trades, vendors and suppliers; research and identify trades and suppliers in all regions we operate.  Review, negotiate and sign various vendor contracts such as janitorial, security, alarms, HVAC, and pest control etc...  Coordinate and support access for installations or service calls such as security, water filtration, shred services, janitorial, etc.  Manage installations, maintenance & removal of alarm and security for all locations. including individual alarm codes for staff and all after hours alarm response calls.  Manage and coordinate preventative and cyclical maintenance such as mechanical, landscaping, snow removal, water filter changes, fire safety, etc.  Contact and liaise between landlords, property managers, and subtenants to address complaints or repairs required.  Approving Facilities invoices in Concur on a weekly recuring basis.  Managing internal departments/external vendors to achieve Facilities department goals and initiatives.  Communicates various events or tasks to internal and external clients via phone or email.  Provide support to Westland renovation and construction project teams.  Manage/update service providers to support new builds, renovations, merge, and acquisitions.  Manage onboarding of new facilities staff. Here's what you bring:  Proven experience in a facilities management role, ideally within a retail/branch organization  High level of experience understanding/reviewing vendor contracts.  Ability to read plans and edit PDF's  Keen Knowledge of all Construction and Repairs  Previous experience in a role managing and consolidating large amounts of information in Excel or Smartsheet  High level of proficiency in MS Office (Excel, Word, Outlook etc.)  Experience with Smartsheets, Service Now and SharePoint is an assett  Excellent organizational and problem-solving skills, and a service-oriented mindset  Excellent time management and the ability to juggle multiple priorities  Strong communication skills including writing and editing  Strong attention to detail and accuracy and demonstrated ability to execute work promptly and efficiently  Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients.  description ---> Property Filed AdjusterWestland Insurance GroupVernon, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONVernon, BCPOSTED4 days agoProperty Filed Adjuster  Vernon, BC, Canada Req #512  Wednesday, April 20, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Property Field Adjuster working remotely and covering claims primarily in Kelowna, Vernon, and surrounding areas. This is a great opportunity and will be a home based position with daily travel required. What we offer:  Competitive salary  Vehicle Allowance  Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programs The Opportunity: As a Property Field Adjuster with Westland, you will be contributing to our goal of delivering an exceptional claims experience to our clients by meeting with them and assisting them through the claims process. In this role you'll: • Investigate commercial lines and personal lines property insurance claims with insureds, third parties and other related parties in order to obtain facts and information  • Review facts, policy coverages, expert reports and case law to make decisions on coverage, claim value and settlement  • Manage and direct Restoration Contractors to ensure best practices are being followed for property restoration, and that costs are in line with work required  • Responsible for data accuracy, issuance of payments to insureds, vendors and other related parties to a claim  • Manage and direct other claim related experts such as Engineers and Legal Counsel  • Responsible for providing exemplary client service and keeping all related parties informed of the claims process and status Here's what you bring: • 5+ years of multi-line adjusting experience, with 2+ years of field work in property claims adjudication  • Insurance Broker Level 2 license and/or CIP designation  • Valid Driver's License  • Community College or University Degree  • Strong background in residential and commercial property insurance  • Ability to work independently with excellent time management and organizational skills  • Effective written and verbal communication abilities  • Good knowledge of building construction and restoration practices  • Computer proficiency with an ability to adapt easily to new computer programs Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process.  position ----> Support Specialist - IT Service Desk
 company ---> Westland Insurance Group
 description ---> Support Specialist - IT Service DeskWestland Insurance GroupSurrey, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONSurrey, BCPOSTED3 days agoSupport Specialist - IT Service Desk Surrey (Head Office), BC, 2121 160th St #200, Surrey, British Columbia, Canada Req #845  Thursday, April 21, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Support Specialist- IT Service Desk in Surrey, BC at our Surrey Head office. This is a great opportunity to join our IT Operations team.What we offer Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programsThe Opportunity: The Support Specialist is an integral member of the IT team and is responsible for ensuring that incidents relating to in-house computing systems are recorded and resolved by means of troubleshooting problems, advising on appropriate actions, or redirecting to appropriate resources using the IT Service Management System. In this role you'll:  Form part of a Service Desk team, acting as a single point of contact to communicate, manage and resolve IT incidents (break/fix) and fulfill service requests  Provide technical phone/email/desk-side support for internal IT customers  Provide level 1 and 2 phone/chat/email/desk-side support for our technology systems  Participate in IT customer projects including office moves, infrastructure deployments, and cloud services  Update, create and maintain support documentation  Add users to a network and assign and update security permissions on the network  Responsible for time allocation/prioritization, task management, and client follow up  Support users on the proper use of hardware and software  Document, track, and monitor tickets in the ticketing system to ensure timely resolution  Work as part of a team in a structured environment with defined targets and deliverables  Ability to prioritize and quickly turnaround escalated / expedited user requests  Ability to set up/modify/remove user access for a wide variety of applications  Troubleshoot/investigate issues related to laptops, desktops, printers, VOIP phones, etc. and liaise with other technical teams to resolve problems  Ability to provide real time support to a wide variety of technology users  Perform other duties as required to deliver exceptional service and support Here's what you bring: Minimum 3 years' experience in a Service Desk role  Experience with ServiceNow is considered a strong asset  Knowledge related to technology/computer science field normally attained through completion of a degree/diploma. Certification in A+, Help Desk Professional, ITIL foundations preferred or an equivalent combination of education, training, and experience  Experience providing user support in a Microsoft Active Directory environment  Proficiency in the use of remote desktop management and support tools  Experience in workstation configuration and support of desktop PCs  Experience in troubleshooting issues for Windows 10, MS Office 2010 and Office 365 and Adobe applications  Ensures process consistency and commitment to customer service excellence  Strong attention to detail and accuracy is a must  Enjoys working in a team environment but also can work independently  Demonstrates analytical, organizational and problem-solving aptitude  Excellent written and verbal communication skills  Ability to learn new technologies quickly  Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process. Manages any change management impacts with the implementation of new programs or initiatives.  Collaborates with other lines of business through reciprocity of referrals to lead to new members, customers, and product sales.  Stays abreast of competitive, environmental and industry trends that may impact marketing position and member satisfaction; sets direction; focuses resources and executes plans to develop and grow the business.  Fosters and maintains strong relationships with Westland's key business partners, primarily, the Insurance companies through which the company writes business.  Maintains a high level of current industry knowledge and actively participates in professional associations related to insurance such as Insurance Brokers Association of BC, staying at the forefront of the profession. Support charitable organizations through company and industry events.  Supports special projects and key initiatives as directed by the Retail Operations leaders.  For new acquisitions, ensures appropriate training and staffing levels to support the. Provides support for salary and benefits harmonization under the guidance of the VP Personal Insurance.  Travel as required. Here's what you bring:  Minimum of 5 years' management / leadership experience.  Demonstrated effective leadership within the insurance industry, applying proactive sales and service environment.  Proven results in developing, coaching and leading a team.  Demonstrated commitment to excellence in the insurance industry and the ability to differentiate Westland in the marketplace.  Demonstrated ability to exceed business results and inspire teams to perform within an extremely competitive environment.  Demonstrated ability to execute tactical plans that link to the operating and strategic plans of the business.  High level of personal and professional integrity with exceptional communication and interpersonal skills.  Post-secondary education in Business Administration, or other related field preferred.  Achieved highest possible P&C Insurance License, working on or achieved CAIB or CIP designation.  description ---> Support Specialist - IT Service DeskWestland Insurance GroupSurrey, BCApplyJOB DETAILSLOCATIONSurrey, BCPOSTED3 days agoSupport Specialist - IT Service Desk Surrey (Head Office), BC, 2121 160th St #200, Surrey, British Columbia, Canada Req #845  Thursday, April 21, 2022 Westland Insurance Group Ltd has an exciting opportunity for a Support Specialist- IT Service Desk in Surrey, BC at our Surrey Head office. This is a great opportunity to join our IT Operations team.What we offer Comprehensive medical and dental benefits  Diverse mix of staff and demonstrated work/life balance  Career growth opportunities and continuing education programsThe Opportunity: The Support Specialist is an integral member of the IT team and is responsible for ensuring that incidents relating to in-house computing systems are recorded and resolved by means of troubleshooting problems, advising on appropriate actions, or redirecting to appropriate resources using the IT Service Management System. In this role you'll:  Form part of a Service Desk team, acting as a single point of contact to communicate, manage and resolve IT incidents (break/fix) and fulfill service requests  Provide technical phone/email/desk-side support for internal IT customers  Provide level 1 and 2 phone/chat/email/desk-side support for our technology systems  Participate in IT customer projects including office moves, infrastructure deployments, and cloud services  Update, create and maintain support documentation  Add users to a network and assign and update security permissions on the network  Responsible for time allocation/prioritization, task management, and client follow up  Support users on the proper use of hardware and software  Document, track, and monitor tickets in the ticketing system to ensure timely resolution  Work as part of a team in a structured environment with defined targets and deliverables  Ability to prioritize and quickly turnaround escalated / expedited user requests  Ability to set up/modify/remove user access for a wide variety of applications  Troubleshoot/investigate issues related to laptops, desktops, printers, VOIP phones, etc. and liaise with other technical teams to resolve problems  Ability to provide real time support to a wide variety of technology users  Perform other duties as required to deliver exceptional service and support Here's what you bring: Minimum 3 years' experience in a Service Desk role  Experience with ServiceNow is considered a strong asset  Knowledge related to technology/computer science field normally attained through completion of a degree/diploma. Certification in A+, Help Desk Professional, ITIL foundations preferred or an equivalent combination of education, training, and experience  Experience providing user support in a Microsoft Active Directory environment  Proficiency in the use of remote desktop management and support tools  Experience in workstation configuration and support of desktop PCs  Experience in troubleshooting issues for Windows 10, MS Office 2010 and Office 365 and Adobe applications  Ensures process consistency and commitment to customer service excellence  Strong attention to detail and accuracy is a must  Enjoys working in a team environment but also can work independently  Demonstrates analytical, organizational and problem-solving aptitude  Excellent written and verbal communication skills  Ability to learn new technologies quickly  Westland Insurance Group is one of the largest and fastest-growing independent property and casualty insurance brokers in Canada. With a national network of 195 locations and over 2,100 employees, the company continues to expand coast to coast. Westland's brokers provide expert advice to home, business, farm, life, and auto insurance clients. Since its founding in 1980, Westland has remained a family-owned company that is committed to supporting its local communities.Westland Insurance Ltd. is an inclusive organization that values diversity in its workforce. We listen, champion equality and diversity, and create safe welcoming spaces where everyone has a voice and is free to be themselves. Westland Insurance Ltd. encourages applications from all qualified individuals and will accommodate applicants' disability-related needs, up to the point of undue hardship, throughout all stages of the recruitment and selection process. This is a great opportunity to help lay the foundation and infrastructure for data analytics inside of a unique organization which is both an insurer and broker. You will strive to understand the data, build out processes for improving the quality of the data and put in place automated core reporting.
